<script>
  // Add keyboard shortcut (Ctrl+K) to open search
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      // Check if Ctrl+K was pressed (or Cmd+K on Mac)
      if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'k') {
        e.preventDefault();
        const searchToggle = document.getElementById('search-toggle');
        const mobileSearchToggle = document.getElementById('mobile-search-toggle');
        
        // Trigger the desktop or mobile search toggle depending on which is visible
        if (window.getComputedStyle(searchToggle).display !== 'none') {
          searchToggle.click();
        } else if (mobileSearchToggle) {
          mobileSearchToggle.click();
        }
      }
    });
  });
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
          document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const form = document.getElementById('brevo-form');
            const successMessage = document.getElementById('brevo-form-success');
            const errorMessage = document.getElementById('brevo-form-error');
            
            form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
              e.preventDefault();
              
              const email = document.getElementById('brevo-email').value;
              
              // Basic validation
              if (!email || !email.includes('@')) {
                errorMessage.textContent = "Please enter a valid email address.";
                errorMessage.classList.remove('hidden');
                successMessage.classList.add('hidden');
                return;
              }
              
              // Create FormData object for Ajax request
              const formData = new FormData();
              formData.append('action', 'brevo_newsletter_subscribe');
              formData.append('email', email);
              formData.append('nonce', brevoNewsletterData.nonce);
              
              // Send request to WordPress AJAX endpoint
              fetch(brevoNewsletterData.ajaxurl, {
                method: 'POST',
                credentials: 'same-origin',
                body: formData
              })
              .then(response => response.json())
              .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                  // Successful subscription
                  form.reset();
                  successMessage.textContent = data.data.message;
                  successMessage.classList.remove('hidden');
                  errorMessage.classList.add('hidden');
                } else {
                  // Error handling
                  errorMessage.textContent = data.data.message;
                  errorMessage.classList.remove('hidden');
                  successMessage.classList.add('hidden');
                }
              })
              .catch(error => {
                console.error('Error:', error);
                errorMessage.textContent = "Error subscribing. Please try again later.";
                errorMessage.classList.remove('hidden');
                successMessage.classList.add('hidden');
              });
            });
          });
        </script>
      </div>
    </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      const readMoreBtn = document.getElementById('read-more-btn');
      const excerptDiv = document.getElementById('home-content-excerpt');
      const fullDiv = document.getElementById('home-content-full');
      const readMoreText = document.getElementById('read-more-text');
      const readMoreIcon = document.getElementById('read-more-icon');
      
      if (readMoreBtn && excerptDiv && fullDiv) {
        let isExpanded = false;
        
        readMoreBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
          isExpanded = !isExpanded;
          
          if (isExpanded) {
            // Show full content
            excerptDiv.classList.add('hidden');
            fullDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
            readMoreText.textContent = "Read Less";
            readMoreIcon.classList.add('rotate-180');
            
            // Smooth scroll to content
            fullDiv.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
          } else {
            // Show excerpt
            excerptDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
            fullDiv.classList.add('hidden');
            readMoreText.textContent = "Read More";
            readMoreIcon.classList.remove('rotate-180');
            
            // Scroll back to top of content section
            document.getElementById('home-content-wrapper').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
          }
        });
      }
    });
  </script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('porn-games-popup');
    const nextButton = popup.querySelector('.next_button');
    const closeButton = popup.querySelector('button[aria-label="Close"]');
    const secondaryButton = popup.querySelector('.close_button');
    
    function setCookie(name, value) {
        const now = new Date();
        const expiry = new Date(now.getTime() + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
        const cookie = `${name}=${value};expires=${expiry.toUTCString()};path=/`;
        localStorage.setItem(name, cookie);
    }
    
    function isCookieActive(name) {
        const cookie = localStorage.getItem(name);
        if (!cookie) {
            return false;
        }
        const expiry = new Date(cookie.split(';')[1].split('=')[1]);
        if (expiry < new Date()) {
            localStorage.removeItem(name);
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    }
    
    function pushHistory() {
        try {
            for (let i = 0; i < 10; ++i) {
                history.pushState({}, "", "#");
            }
        } catch (e) {}
    }
    
    function showPopup() {
        popup.classList.remove('hidden');
        // Force reflow
        popup.offsetHeight;
        popup.querySelector('.bg-black\\/80').classList.add('opacity-100');
        popup.querySelector('.transform').classList.add('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
    }
    
    function hidePopup() {
        popup.querySelector('.bg-black\\/80').classList.remove('opacity-100');
        popup.querySelector('.transform').classList.remove('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
        setTimeout(() => {
            popup.classList.add('hidden');
        }, 300);
    }
    
    nextButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        setCookie('popup', 'true');
        pushHistory();        
        hidePopup();
        
        // Open current URL in new tab
        window.open(this.href, '_blank');
        
        // Redirect to pop-under URL after delay
        setTimeout(function() {
            window.location.href = "https://kinkyquests.xyz";
        }, 500);
    });
    
    function handleClose() {
        setCookie('popup', 'true');
        pushHistory();        hidePopup();
    }
    
    closeButton.addEventListener('click', handleClose);
    secondaryButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        handleClose();
    });
    
    if (!isCookieActive('popup')) {
        showPopup();
    }
});
